<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

好的，我了解了任务内容。让我总结一下：

## 底部手势识别逻辑错误 - 任务理解

**问题描述**：
当前代码使用手势的物理位置 (`location.y > screenHeight - 300`) 来判断是否触发底部切换，这导致只有在屏幕最底部滑动时才会响应。正确的逻辑应该基于 `FlexScrollView` 的滚动状态：当用户滚动到最底部后继续向下拖拽（overscroll）时触发 `Switch bar → FilterCapsuleBar` 切换。

**当前错误代码**（`PhotoViewController+Filter.swift` 第 357-376 行）：
```swift
let location = pan.location(in: view)
let isInBottomArea = location.y > screenHeight - 300  // ❌ 仅屏幕物理位置判断
```

**正确逻辑**：
```swift
// 基于 FlexScrollView 滚动状态
let offsetY = gridView.flexScrollView.contentOffset.y
let maxOffset = gridView.flexScrollView.contentSize.height - bounds.height
let isAtBottom = offsetY >= maxOffset - 5  // ✅ 滚动到底部
```

**修复方案**：
1. 在 `PhotoViewController+Filter.swift` 添加 `isAtBottom/isNearBottom` 计算属性，基于 `gridView.flexScrollView.contentOffset`
2. 修改 `gestureRecognizerShouldBegin` - 返回 `isAtBottom && isVertical && translation.y > 0`
3. 实现 `UIScrollViewDelegate` 监听滚动，处理从底部向上滑动恢复 Switch bar


4. 修改 `shouldRecognizeSimultaneouslyWith` - 允许 `bottomPanGesture` 与 `flexScrollView.panGestureRecognizer` 同时识别
5. 在 `viewDidLoad` 中调用 `setupScrollViewMonitoring()` 初始化监听

涉及的组件包括 `gridView: FlexGridView`、`bottomPanGesture: UIPanGestureRecognizer` 和 `filterCoordinator: HomeFilterCoordinator`，这些组件共同控制从 `TabSwitcher` 到 `FilterCapsuleBar` 再到 `FilterPanel` 的切换逻辑。

确认我对这个 bug 修复任务的理解正确吗？

</details>

我已阅读任务，以下是我对 **底部filter手势识别逻辑错误** 的理解：

---

## 任务理解确认

### 问题本质
当前代码使用**手势物理位置** (`location.y > screenHeight - 300`) 判断是否触发底部切换，导致只有用户在屏幕最底部滑动时才响应。

### 正确逻辑
应基于 **FlexScrollView 的滚动状态**：用户滚动到**最底部后继续向下拖拽**（overscroll）时才触发 `Switch bar → FilterCapsuleBar` 切换。

### 修复方案要点
1. **添加 `isAtBottom` 计算属性** - 基于 `gridView.flexScrollView.contentOffset.y`
2. **修改 `gestureRecognizerShouldBegin`** - 使用 `isAtBottom && isVertical && translation.y > 0`
3. **实现 `UIScrollViewDelegate`** - 监听滚动，处理从底部向上滑动恢复 Switch bar
4. **修改手势冲突处理** - 允许 `bottomPanGesture` 与 `flexScrollView.panGestureRecognizer` 同时识别
5. **初始化监听** - 在 `viewDidLoad` 中调用 `setupScrollViewMonitoring()`

### 涉及组件
- `gridView: FlexGridView` (含 `flexScrollView`)
- `bottomPanGesture: UIPanGestureRecognizer`
- `filterCoordinator: HomeFilterCoordinator`
- `TabSwitcher` ↔ `FilterCapsuleBar` ↔ `FilterPanel`

---

我理解正确吗？确认后我将开始修复代码。

    89	    private func setupBottomPanGesture() {
    90	        let pan = UIPanGestureRecognizer(target: self, action: #selector(handleBottomPan(_:)))
    91	        pan.delegate = self
    92	        
    93	        // 【关键日志】添加到视图前检查
    94	        print("[FILTER] 准备添加手势识别器, view.bounds: \(view.bounds)")
    95	        
    96	        // 添加到视图（覆盖底部区域）
    97	        view.addGestureRecognizer(pan)
    98	        bottomPanGesture = pan
    99	        
   100	        // 【关键日志】确认添加成功
   101	        print("[FILTER] ✅ 底部手势识别器已添加")
   102	    }
   103	    
   104	    @objc private func handleBottomPan(_ gesture: UIPanGestureRecognizer) {
   105	        let translation = gesture.translation(in: view)
   106	        let velocity = gesture.velocity(in: view)
   107	        let location = gesture.location(in: view)
   108	        
   109	        // 【日志】只记录底部区域的手势
   110	        let screenHeight = view.bounds.height
   111	        let isInBottomArea = location.y > screenHeight - 150
   112	        
   113	        print("[FILTER] 手势 state:\(gesture.state.rawValue) dy:\(translation.y) locationY:\(location.y) isBottom:\(isInBottomArea)")
   114	        
   115	        // 只有在底部区域的手势才处理
   116	        guard isInBottomArea else { return }
   117	        
   118	        print("[FILTER] ✅ 在底部区域，传递给 coordinator")
   119	        
   120	        filterCoordinator?.handleBottomPanGesture(
   121	            translation: translation,
   122	            velocity: velocity,
   123	            state: gesture.state
   124	        )
   125	    }
   126	    
   127	    // MARK: - 过滤结果更新
   128	    func applyFilterResult(_ result: HomeFilterResult) {
   129	        // 计算差量更新
   130	        let oldAssets = self.displayAssets
   131	        let newAssets = result.filteredAssets
   132	        
   133	        // 更新数据源
   134	        self.displayAssets = newAssets
   135	        
   136	        // 使用 FlexGridView 的差量更新
   137	        performDiffUpdate(oldAssets: oldAssets, newAssets: newAssets)
   138	        
   139	        // 更新胶囊条
   140	        updateCapsuleBar(with: result)
   141	        
   142	        // 更新空状态
   143	        updateEmptyState(with: result)
   144	    }
   145	    
   146	    private func performDiffUpdate(oldAssets: [AssetModel], newAssets: [AssetModel]) {
   147	        // 计算差异
   148	        let oldSet = Set(oldAssets.map { $0.assetId })
   149	        let newSet = Set(newAssets.map { $0.assetId })
   150	        
   151	        let deletedIds = oldSet.subtracting(newSet)
   152	        let insertedIds = newSet.subtracting(oldSet)
   153	        
   154	        // 转换为 IndexPath
   155	        let deletions = oldAssets.enumerated()
   156	            .filter { deletedIds.contains($0.element.assetId) }
   157	            .map { IndexPath(item: $0.offset, section: 0) }
   158	        
   159	        let insertions = newAssets.enumerated()
   160	            .filter { insertedIds.contains($0.element.assetId) }
   161	            .map { IndexPath(item: $0.offset, section: 0) }
   162	        
   163	        // 批量更新（使用 FlexGridView 的公开 API）
   164	        // 注意：必须先更新数据源，再调用删除/插入方法
   165	        if !deletions.isEmpty {
   166	            gridView.deleteItems(at: deletions, animated: true)
   167	        }
   168	        if !insertions.isEmpty {
   169	            let insertionsWithCount = insertions.map { ($0, 1) }
   170	            gridView.insertItems(at: insertionsWithCount, animated: true)
   171	        }
   172	    }
   173	    
   174	    private func updateCapsuleBar(with result: HomeFilterResult) {
   175	        guard let capsuleBar = filterCapsuleBar else { return }
   176	        
   177	        if result.hasActiveFilters {
   178	            capsuleBar.configure(
   179	                capsules: result.conditionCapsules,
   180	                onExpand: { [weak self] in
   181	                    self?.filterCoordinator?.switchToExpandedMode()
   182	                },
   183	                onCapsuleTap: { [weak self] condition in
   184	                    // 点击胶囊可以跳转到展开态编辑
   185	                    self?.filterCoordinator?.switchToExpandedMode()
   186	                },
   187	                onCapsuleClose: { [weak self] condition in
   188	                    self?.filterCoordinator?.clearCondition(condition)
   189	                }
   190	            )
   191	        } else {
   192	            // 显示快捷按钮
   193	            capsuleBar.showQuickButtons(
   194	                onPhotos: { [weak self] in
   195	                    self?.filterCoordinator?.updateMediaType(.image)
   196	                },
   197	                onVideos: { [weak self] in
   198	                    self?.filterCoordinator?.updateMediaType(.video)
   199	                },
   200	                onAll: { [weak self] in
   201	                    self?.filterCoordinator?.switchToBrowsingMode()
   202	                }
   203	            )
   204	        }
   205	    }
   206	    
   207	    private func updateEmptyState(with result: HomeFilterResult) {
   208	        guard let emptyStateView = filterEmptyStateView else { return }
   209	        
   210	        if let reason = result.emptyStateReason {
   211	            emptyStateView.configure(reason: reason) { [weak self] in
   212	                self?.filterCoordinator?.clearAllConditions()
   213	            }
   214	            emptyStateView.alpha = 1
   215	        } else {
   216	            emptyStateView.alpha = 0
   217	        }
   218	    }
   219	    
   220	    // MARK: - 底部模式切换动画
   221	    func animateToBottomMode(_ mode: HomeBottomMode) {
   222	        guard let capsuleBar = filterCapsuleBar,
   223	              let panel = filterPanel else { return }
   224	        
   225	        switch mode {
   226	        case .browsing:
   227	            // 隐藏胶囊条和面板，显示 TabSwitcher
   228	            capsuleBar.animateOut()
   229	            panel.animateOut(to: view.bounds.height) { [weak self] in
   230	                panel.alpha = 0
   231	            }
   232	            
   233	        case .filterCollapsed:
   234	            // 显示胶囊条，隐藏面板
   235	            panel.animateOut(to: view.bounds.height) {
   236	                panel.alpha = 0
   237	            }
   238	            capsuleBar.alpha = 1
   239	            capsuleBar.animateIn()
   240	            
   241	        case .filterExpanded:
   242	            // 显示面板，隐藏胶囊条
   243	            capsuleBar.alpha = 0
   244	            panel.alpha = 1
   245	            panel.animateIn(from: view.bounds.height)
   246	        }
   247	    }
   248	    
   249	    // MARK: - 长按快捷卡片
   250	    func showQuickActionCard(_ content: QuickActionCardContent, at indexPath: IndexPath) {
   251	        let cardView = QuickActionCardView()
   252	        
   253	        // 获取照片在屏幕中的位置（使用公开的 itemFrame API）
   254	        let itemIndexPath = IndexPath(item: indexPath.item, section: indexPath.section)
   255	        guard let cellFrame = gridView.itemFrame(index: itemIndexPath, level: gridView.currentLevel) else { return }
   256	        let windowFrame = gridView.convert(cellFrame, to: nil)
   257	        
   258	        cardView.configure(
   259	            content: content,
   260	            onAction: { [weak self] action in
   261	                self?.filterCoordinator?.executeQuickAction(action, for: content.asset)
   262	                cardView.dismiss()
   263	            },
   264	            onDismiss: { }
   265	        )
   266	        
   267	        cardView.show(from: windowFrame, in: view)
   268	    }
   269	}
   270	
   271	// MARK: - HomeFilterCoordinatorDelegate
   272	
   273	extension PhotoViewController: HomeFilterCoordinatorDelegate {
   274	    func coordinator(
   275	        _ coordinator: HomeFilterCoordinator,
   276	        didUpdateResult result: HomeFilterResult
   277	    ) {
   278	        applyFilterResult(result)
   279	    }
   280	    
   281	    func coordinator(
   282	        _ coordinator: HomeFilterCoordinator,
   283	        didChangeBottomMode mode: HomeBottomMode
   284	    ) {
   285	        animateToBottomMode(mode)
   286	    }
   287	    
   288	    func coordinator(
   289	        _ coordinator: HomeFilterCoordinator,
   290	        showQuickAction content: QuickActionCardContent,
   291	        for asset: AssetModel,

   293	    ) {
   294	        showQuickActionCard(content, at: indexPath)
   295	    }

   354	// MARK: - UIGestureRecognizerDelegate
   355	
   356	extension PhotoViewController: UIGestureRecognizerDelegate {
   357	    public func gestureRecognizerShouldBegin(_ gestureRecognizer: UIGestureRecognizer) -> Bool {
   358	        // 【关键日志】所有手势的开始都会记录
   359	        print("[FILTER] gestureRecognizerShouldBegin: \(type(of: gestureRecognizer))")
   360	        
   361	        if gestureRecognizer === bottomPanGesture {
   362	            guard let pan = gestureRecognizer as? UIPanGestureRecognizer else { return true }
   363	            
   364	            let translation = pan.translation(in: view)
   365	            let location = pan.location(in: view)
   366	            let screenHeight = view.bounds.height
   367	            let isInBottomArea = location.y > screenHeight - 150
   368	            let isVertical = abs(translation.y) > abs(translation.x)
   369	            
   370	            print("[FILTER] 👆 底部手势判断: isBottom:\(isInBottomArea) isVertical:\(isVertical)")
   371	            
   372	            // 只在底部区域且垂直滑动时开始
   373	            return isInBottomArea && isVertical
   374	        }
   375	        return true
   376	    }
   377	    
   378	    public func gestureRecognizer(_ gestureRecognizer: UIGestureRecognizer, shouldRecognizeSimultaneouslyWith otherGestureRecognizer: UIGestureRecognizer) -> Bool {
   379	        // 【日志】手势同时识别判断
   380	        Logger.log("filter", subsystem: "com.photomanager.homefilter") {
   381	            "[PhotoViewController] shouldRecognizeSimultaneouslyWith: \(type(of: otherGestureRecognizer))"
   382	        }
   383	        // 不与任何其他手势同时识别，避免冲突
   384	        return false
   385	    }
   386	}

   158	            make.width.height.equalTo(buttonSize)
   159	            make.trailing.equalToSuperview().offset(-rightMargin)
   160	            make.bottom.equalTo(view.safeAreaLayoutGuide).offset(-4)
   161	        }
   162

   164	            make.width.height.equalTo(buttonSize)

   166	            make.bottom.equalTo(trashButton)

    37	/// 首页过滤协调器
    38	///
    39	/// @MainActor 保证所有 UI 相关操作在主线程
    40	@MainActor
    41	public final class HomeFilterCoordinator {
    42	    
    43	    // MARK: - 日志
    44	    private static let subsystem = "com.photomanager.homefilter"
    45	    
    46	    // MARK: - 依赖
    47	    private let indexProvider: HomeFilterIndexProvider
    48	    private let engine: HomeFilterEngine
    49	    private let preferenceStore: HomeFilterPreferenceStore
    50	    private let actionResolver: QuickActionResolver
    51	    private let stateMachine: HomeBottomStateMachine
    52

    54	    public weak var delegate: HomeFilterCoordinatorDelegate?
    55	    public weak var chromeHost: PhotoBottomChromeHost?
    56	    
    57	    /// 当前过滤状态（只读）
    58	    public private(set) var currentState: HomeFilterState {
    59	        didSet {
    60	            Logger.log("state", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { 
    61	                "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 过滤状态变化" 
    62	            }
    63	        }
    64	    }
    65	    
    66	    /// 当前底部模式（只读）
    67	    public private(set) var bottomMode: HomeBottomMode {
    68	        didSet {
    69	            if oldValue != bottomMode {
    70	                Logger.log("state", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { 
    71	                    "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 底部模式变化: \(oldValue) → \(bottomMode)" 
    72	                }
    73	                delegate?.coordinator(self, didChangeBottomMode: bottomMode)
    74	                updateTabSwitcherVisibility()
    75	            }
    76	        }
    77	    }
    78	    
    79	    /// 当前过滤结果（只读）
    80	    public private(set) var currentResult: HomeFilterResult?
    81	    
    82	    /// 当前快照（用于快捷卡片解析）
    83	    private var currentSnapshot: HomeFilterInputSnapshot?
    84	    
    85	    /// 计算任务，用于取消
    86	    private var calculationTask: Task<Void, Never>?
    87	    
    88	    // MARK: - 初始化
    89	    public init(
    90	        indexProvider: HomeFilterIndexProvider,
    91	        engine: HomeFilterEngine,
    92	        preferenceStore: HomeFilterPreferenceStore = .shared,
    93	        actionResolver: QuickActionResolver = .init()
    94	    ) {
    95	        self.indexProvider = indexProvider
    96	        self.engine = engine
    97	        self.preferenceStore = preferenceStore
    98	        self.actionResolver = actionResolver
    99	        self.stateMachine = HomeBottomStateMachine(initialMode: .browsing)
   100	        self.currentState = HomeFilterState()
   101	        self.bottomMode = .browsing
   102	        
   103	        self.stateMachine.delegate = self
   104	        
   105	        Logger.log("init", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 初始化完成" }
   106	    }
   107	    
   108	    // MARK: - 状态操作
   109	    
   110	    /// 更新媒体类型
   111	    public func updateMediaType(_ type: MediaFilterType) {
   112	        guard currentState.mediaType != type else { return }
   113	        currentState.mediaType = type
   114	        
   115	        // 媒体类型变化时可能需要状态清洗
   116	        if type == .video {
   117	            // 自动清除不兼容条件
   118	            currentState.contentConditions = [:]
   119	            currentState.organizationRules.remove(.hideJunkPhotos)
   120	            currentState.organizationRules.remove(.collapseSimilarPhotos)
   121	        }
   122	        
   123	        triggerRecalculation()
   124	    }
   125	    
   126	    /// 更新人物条件
   127	    public func updatePersonCondition(_ condition: FilterTriState, for clusterId: Int64) {
   128	        switch condition {
   129	        case .neutral:
   130	            currentState.personConditions.removeValue(forKey: clusterId)
   131	            // 如果取消的是单人聚焦的人物，清除聚焦模式
   132	            if case .singlePerson(let focusId) = currentState.personFocusMode,
   133	               focusId == clusterId {
   134	                currentState.personFocusMode = .none
   135	            }
   136	        case .include, .exclude:
   137	            currentState.personConditions[clusterId] = condition
   138	        }
   139	        triggerRecalculation()
   140	    }
   141	    
   142	    /// 进入"只看此人"模式（清除其他人物条件）
   143	    public func enterSinglePersonFocusMode(clusterId: Int64) {
   144	        // 清除所有其他人物条件
   145	        currentState.personConditions = [clusterId: .include]
   146	        currentState.personFocusMode = .singlePerson(clusterId: clusterId)
   147	        
   148	        // 清除不兼容条件（单人聚焦模式清洗）
   149	        currentState.contentConditions = [:]
   150	        currentState.organizationRules.remove(.hideJunkPhotos)
   151	        // collapseSimilarPhotos 保留（PRD: 允许继续清理该人物的模糊/相似照片）
   152	        
   153	        triggerRecalculation()
   154	    }
   155	    
   156	    /// 更新内容条件
   157	    public func updateContentCondition(_ condition: FilterTriState, for key: HomeContentKey) {
   158	        // 检查当前模式是否允许
   159	        if case .singlePerson = currentState.personFocusMode {
   160	            // 单人聚焦模式下不允许内容类别（模糊除外，但 V1.0 只有截图）
   161	            Logger.log("state", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { 
   162	                "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 单人聚焦模式下禁止设置内容条件" 
   163	            }
   164	            return
   165	        }
   166	        
   167	        switch condition {
   168	        case .neutral:
   169	            currentState.contentConditions.removeValue(forKey: key)
   170	        case .include, .exclude:
   171	            currentState.contentConditions[key] = condition
   172	        }
   173	        triggerRecalculation()
   174	    }
   175	    
   176	    /// 切换整理规则
   177	    public func toggleOrganizationRule(_ rule: HomeOrganizationRule) {
   178	        // 检查当前模式是否允许
   179	        if currentState.mediaType == .video {
   180	            // 视频模式下整理规则不可用
   181	            Logger.log("state", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { 
   182	                "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 视频模式下禁止设置整理规则" 
   183	            }
   184	            return
   185	        }
   186	        
   187	        if currentState.organizationRules.contains(rule) {
   188	            currentState.organizationRules.remove(rule)
   189	        } else {
   190	            currentState.organizationRules.insert(rule)
   191	        }
   192	        triggerRecalculation()
   193	    }
   194	    
   195	    /// 清除所有条件
   196	    public func clearAllConditions() {
   197	        Logger.log("state", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 清除所有条件" }
   198	        
   199	        currentState = HomeFilterState()
   200	        triggerRecalculation()
   201	        
   202	        // 如果没有生效条件，回到浏览态
   203	        if !hasActiveConditions {
   204	            switchToBrowsingMode()
   205	        }
   206	    }
   207	    
   208	    /// 清除指定条件
   209	    public func clearCondition(_ condition: FilterCondition) {
   210	        Logger.log("state", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 清除条件: \(condition)" }
   211	        
   212	        switch condition {
   213	        case .mediaType(let type):
   214	            // 媒体类型只能重置为 all
   215	            if currentState.mediaType == type {
   216	                currentState.mediaType = .all
   217	            }
   218	        case .person(let id):
   219	            currentState.personConditions.removeValue(forKey: id)
   220	            // 如果清除的是单人聚焦的人物，清除聚焦模式
   221	            if case .singlePerson(let focusId) = currentState.personFocusMode,
   222	               focusId == id {
   223	                currentState.personFocusMode = .none
   224	            }
   225	        case .content(let key):
   226	            currentState.contentConditions.removeValue(forKey: key)
   227	        case .organization(let rule):
   228	            currentState.organizationRules.remove(rule)
   229	        }
   230	        triggerRecalculation()
   231	    }
   232	    
   233	    // MARK: - 底部模式切换
   234	    
   235	    public func switchToBrowsingMode() {
   236	        stateMachine.switchToBrowsing()
   237	    }
   238	    
   239	    public func switchToCollapsedMode(fromManualTrigger: Bool = false) {
   240	        // 检查是否需要首次预置
   241	        if fromManualTrigger {
   242	            handleInitialPresetIfNeeded()
   243	        }
   244	        stateMachine.switchToCollapsed()
   245	    }
   246	    
   247	    public func switchToExpandedMode() {
   248	        stateMachine.switchToExpanded()
   249	    }
   250	    
   251	    /// 处理底部上滑手势
   252	    public func handleBottomPanGesture(
   253	        translation: CGPoint,
   254	        velocity: CGPoint = .zero,
   255	        state: UIGestureRecognizer.State
   256	    ) {
   257	        stateMachine.handlePan(translation: translation, velocity: velocity, gestureState: state)
   258	    }
   259	    
   260	    // MARK: - 快捷动作
   261	    
   262	    /// 处理照片长按
   263	    public func handleLongPress(on asset: AssetModel, at indexPath: IndexPath) {
   264	        Logger.log("action", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { 
   265	            "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 处理长按: \(asset.assetId)" 
   266	        }
   267	        
   268	        guard let snapshot = currentSnapshot else {
   269	            Logger.log("error", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { 
   270	                "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 快照未准备好，无法显示快捷卡片" 
   271	            }
   272	            return
   273	        }
   274	        
   275	        let content = actionResolver.resolve(
   276	            asset: asset,
   277	            currentState: currentState,
   278	            indexSnapshot: snapshot
   279	        )
   280	        
   281	        delegate?.coordinator(
   282	            self,
   283	            showQuickAction: content,
   284	            for: asset,
   285	            at: indexPath
   286	        )
   287	    }
   288	    
   289	    /// 执行快捷动作
   290	    public func executeQuickAction(_ action: QuickAction, for asset: AssetModel) {
   291	        Logger.log("action", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { 
   292	            "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 执行快捷动作: \(action)" 
   293	        }
   294	        
   295	        switch action {
   296	        case .viewOnlyContent(let key):
   297	            updateContentCondition(.include, for: key)
   298	            ensureInFilterMode()
   299	            
   300	        case .excludeContent(let key):
   301	            updateContentCondition(.exclude, for: key)
   302	            ensureInFilterMode()
   303	            
   304	        case .viewOnlyPerson(let clusterId):
   305	            enterSinglePersonFocusMode(clusterId: clusterId)
   306	            ensureInFilterMode()
   307	            
   308	        case .excludePerson(let clusterId):
   309	            updatePersonCondition(.exclude, for: clusterId)
   310	            ensureInFilterMode()
   311	            
   312	        case .clearCondition(let condition):
   313	            clearCondition(condition)
   314	            
   315	        case .moveToTrash, .enterMultiSelect:
   316	            // 不修改过滤状态，由 PhotoViewController 处理
   317	            break
   318	        }
   319	    }
   320	    
   321	    // MARK: - 生命周期
   322	    
   323	    public func viewWillAppear() {
   324	        Logger.log("lifecycle", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { "[HomeFilterCoordinator] viewWillAppear" }
   325	        
   326	        // 检查是否需要重算
   327	        Task {
   328	            do {
   329	                try await refreshSnapshotAndRecalculate()
   330	            } catch {
   331	                Logger.log("error", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { 
   332	                    "[HomeFilterCoordinator] viewWillAppear 刷新失败: \(error.localizedDescription)" 
   333	                }
   334	            }
   335	        }
   336	    }
   337	    
   338	    public func viewWillDisappear() {
   339	        Logger.log("lifecycle", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { "[HomeFilterCoordinator] viewWillDisappear" }
   340	        
   341	        calculationTask?.cancel()
   342	    }
   343	    
   344	    /// 处理资产被删除
   345	    public func handleAssetHidden(at index: Int) {
   346	        Logger.log("lifecycle", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { 
   347	            "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 处理资产删除: index=\(index)" 
   348	        }
   349	        
   350	        // 触发重算，条件可能失效
   351	        triggerRecalculation()
   352	    }
   353	    
   354	    /// 处理资产被恢复
   355	    public func handleAssetsRestored() {
   356	        Logger.log("lifecycle", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 处理资产恢复" }
   357	        
   358	        triggerRecalculation()
   359	    }
   360	    
   361	    /// 重新计算结果
   362	    public func recalculateResults() {
   363	        Logger.log("lifecycle", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 手动触发重算" }
   364	        
   365	        triggerRecalculation()
   366	    }
   367	    
   368	    // MARK: - 私有方法
   369	    
   370	    private func triggerRecalculation() {
   371	        calculationTask?.cancel()
   372	        
   373	        calculationTask = Task { [weak self] in
   374	            guard let self = self else { return }
   375	            
   376	            do {
   377	                // 确保有快照
   378	                if self.currentSnapshot == nil {
   379	                    self.currentSnapshot = try await self.indexProvider.buildSnapshot()
   380	                }
   381	                
   382	                guard let snapshot = self.currentSnapshot else { return }
   383	                
   384	                // 在 Engine Actor 中计算
   385	                let result = await self.engine.calculateResult(
   386	                    state: self.currentState,
   387	                    snapshot: snapshot
   388	                )
   389	                
   390	                // 检查是否被取消
   391	                guard !Task.isCancelled else {
   392	                    Logger.log("calculation", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { 
   393	                        "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 计算任务被取消" 
   394	                    }
   395	                    return
   396	                }
   397	                
   398	                self.currentResult = result
   399	                self.delegate?.coordinator(self, didUpdateResult: result)
   400	                
   401	                Logger.log("calculation", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { 
   402	                    "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 计算完成: \(result.filteredAssets.count) 个结果" 
   403	                }
   404	                
   405	            } catch {
   406	                Logger.log("error", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { 
   407	                    "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 计算失败: \(error.localizedDescription)" 
   408	                }
   409	            }
   410	        }
   411	    }
   412	    
   413	    private func refreshSnapshotAndRecalculate() async throws {
   414	        currentSnapshot = try await indexProvider.buildSnapshot()
   415	        triggerRecalculation()
   416	    }
   417	    
   418	    private func updateTabSwitcherVisibility() {
   419	        let shouldHide = bottomMode != .browsing
   420	        chromeHost?.setTabSwitcherHidden(shouldHide, animated: true)
   421	    }
   422	    
   423	    private func handleInitialPresetIfNeeded() {
   424	        // 检查是否首次手动进入过滤态
   425	        guard !preferenceStore.hasConsumedInitialManualPreset else { return }
   426	        
   427	        Logger.log("preset", subsystem: Self.subsystem) { 
   428	            "[HomeFilterCoordinator] 应用首次预置规则" 
   429	        }
   430	        
   431	        // 标记已消费
   432	        preferenceStore.markInitialPresetConsumed()
   433	        
   434	        // 预置规则
   435	        currentState.organizationRules.insert(.hideJunkPhotos)
   436	        currentState.organizationRules.insert(.collapseSimilarPhotos)
   437	        
   438	        // 显示引导提示（由 delegate 处理）
   439	        delegate?.coordinatorShouldShowInitialPresetGuide(self)
   440	    }
   441	    
   442	    private func ensureInFilterMode() {
   443	        if bottomMode == .browsing {
   444	            switchToCollapsedMode()
   445	        }
   446	    }
   447	    
   448	    private var hasActiveConditions: Bool {
   449	        currentState.mediaType != .all ||
   450	        !currentState.personConditions.isEmpty ||
   451	        !currentState.contentConditions.isEmpty ||
   452	        !currentState.organizationRules.isEmpty
   453	    }
   454	}
   455	
   456	// MARK: - HomeBottomStateMachineDelegate
   457	
   458	extension HomeFilterCoordinator: HomeBottomStateMachineDelegate {
   459	    public func stateMachine(
   460	        _ machine: HomeBottomStateMachine,
   461	        didTransition from: HomeBottomMode,
   462	        to: HomeBottomMode
   463	    ) {
   464	        self.bottomMode = to
   465	    }
   466	    
   467	    public func stateMachine(
   468	        _ machine: HomeBottomStateMachine,
   469	        shouldTransitionTo mode: HomeBottomMode
   470	    ) -> Bool {
   471	        // 可以在这里添加拦截逻辑
   472	        // 例如：展开态时如果正在加载，阻止收起
   473	        return true
   474	    }
   475	}
   476	
   477	// MARK: - QuickAction 描述
   478	
   479	extension QuickAction: CustomStringConvertible {
   480	    public var description: String {
   481	        switch self {
   482	        case .viewOnlyContent(let key):
   483	            return "viewOnlyContent(\(key))"
   484	        case .excludeContent(let key):
   485	            return "excludeContent(\(key))"
   486	        case .viewOnlyPerson(let id):
   487	            return "viewOnlyPerson(\(id))"
   488	        case .excludePerson(let id):
   489	            return "excludePerson(\(id))"
   490	        case .clearCondition(let condition):
   491	            return "clearCondition(\(condition))"
   492	        case .moveToTrash:
   493	            return "moveToTrash"
   494	        case .enterMultiSelect:
   495	            return "enterMultiSelect"
   496	        }
   497	    }

     1	//
     2	//  PhotoViewController+FlexGridView.swift
     3	//  PhotoProject
     4	//
     5	//  Created by MC on 2026/1/1.
     6	//
     7	
     8	import Foundation
     9	import UIKit
    10	import FlexGridView
    11	import Photos
    12	import SnapKit
    13	import Utils
    14	
    15	extension PhotoViewController {
    16	    func prepareDisplayAssets(_ assets:[AssetModel]) {
    17	        displayAssets = assets
    18	        
    19	        // 注册数据变化监听者
    20	        dataChangeObserverToken = AssetModelManager.shared.registerDataChangeObserver { [weak self] deleted, added in
    21	            guard let self = self else { return }
    22	            
    23	            // 如果当前 displayAssets 为空且有新增，说明是首次加载，需要 reload 并滚动到底部
    24	            if self.displayAssets.isEmpty && !added.isEmpty {
    25	                self.firstLoad()
    26	            } else {
    27	                self.assetChanged(deleted: deleted, add: added)
    28	            }
    29	        }
    30	    }
    31	    
    32	    private func firstLoad() {
    33	        let (displayAssets, _) = AssetModelManager.shared.assetsByVisibility(currentFilter, sortOrder: sortOrder)
    34	        self.displayAssets = displayAssets
    35	        DispatchQueue.main.async {
    36	            self.gridView.reloadData()
    37	            self.gridView.scrollToBottom()
    38	            self.loadCurrentScreenImage()
    39	        }
    40	    }
    41	    
    42	    private func assetChanged( deleted: [AssetModel], add:[AssetModel]) {
    43	        DispatchQueue.main.async { [weak self] in
    44	            guard let self = self else { return }
    45	            
    46	            // 业务层决定是否使用动画：如果同时添加和删除，不使用动画（避免动画冲突）
    47	            // 否则，默认使用动画（用户操作通常需要动画反馈）
    48	            let shouldAnimate = !(!deleted.isEmpty && !add.isEmpty)
    49	            
    50	            // 处理删除
    51	            if !deleted.isEmpty {
    52	                // 找到要删除的 assets 在 displayAssets 中的索引
    53	                var deleteIndexPaths: [IndexPath] = []
    54	                var indicesToRemove: [Int] = []
    55	                
    56	                for (index, asset) in self.displayAssets.enumerated().reversed() {
    57	                    if deleted.contains(where: { $0.id == asset.id }) {
    58	                        deleteIndexPaths.append(IndexPath(item: index, section: 0))
    59	                        indicesToRemove.append(index)
    60	                    }
    61	                }
    62	                
    63	                // 从 displayAssets 中移除
    64	                for index in indicesToRemove.sorted(by: >) {
    65	                    self.displayAssets.remove(at: index)
    66	                }
    67	                
    68	                // 更新 UI
    69	                if !deleteIndexPaths.isEmpty {
    70	                    self.gridView.deleteItems(at: deleteIndexPaths, animated: shouldAnimate)
    71	                }
    72	            }
    73	            
    74	            // 处理添加
    75	            if !add.isEmpty {
    76	                let sortedAddedAssets = add.sorted {
    77	                    switch self.sortOrder {
    78	                    case .createdAscending:
    79	                        if $0.created != $1.created { return $0.created < $1.created }
    80	                    case .createdDescending:
    81	                        if $0.created != $1.created { return $0.created > $1.created }
    82	                    }
    83	                    return $0.id < $1.id
    84	                }
    85	                
    86	                // 先找到所有插入位置（使用统一的排序方法）
    87	                var insertPositions: [(Int, AssetModel)] = []
    88	                
    89	                for asset in sortedAddedAssets {
    90	                    // 使用统一的排序方法查找插入位置
    91	                    let insertIndex = AssetModelManager.shared.findInsertIndex(
    92	                        for: asset,
    93	                        in: self.displayAssets,
    94	                        sortOrder: self.sortOrder
    95	                    )
    96	                    insertPositions.append((insertIndex, asset))
    97	                }
    98	                
    99	                // 按位置从大到小排序，避免插入后索引变化；同位置按排序规则反向插入
   100	                insertPositions.sort { lhs, rhs in
   101	                    if lhs.0 != rhs.0 { return lhs.0 > rhs.0 }
   102	                    if lhs.1.created != rhs.1.created {
   103	                        switch self.sortOrder {
   104	                        case .createdAscending:
   105	                            return lhs.1.created > rhs.1.created
   106	                        case .createdDescending:
   107	                            return lhs.1.created < rhs.1.created
   108	                        }
   109	                    }
   110	                    return lhs.1.id > rhs.1.id
   111	                }
   112	                
   113	                // 从大到小插入到 displayAssets
   114	                for (insertIndex, asset) in insertPositions {
   115	                    self.displayAssets.insert(asset, at: insertIndex)
   116	                }
   117	                
   118	                // 转换为 FlexGridView 需要的格式（合并同位置的插入）
   119	                var insertCounts: [Int: Int] = [:]
   120	                for (insertIndex, _) in insertPositions {
   121	                    insertCounts[insertIndex, default: 0] += 1
   122	                }
   123	                let indexPathsWithCounts = insertCounts
   124	                    .map { (IndexPath(item: $0.key, section: 0), $0.value) }
   125	                    .sorted { $0.0.item < $1.0.item }
   126	                
   127	                // 更新 UI
   128	                if !indexPathsWithCounts.isEmpty {
   129	                    self.gridView.insertItems(at: indexPathsWithCounts, animated: shouldAnimate)
   130	                }
   131	            }
   132	        }
   133	    }
   134	}
   135	
   136	// MARK: - FlexGridViewDataSource
   137	extension PhotoViewController: FlexGridViewDataSource {
   138	    func sectionCount(in gridView: FlexGridView) -> Int {
   139	        return 1
   140	    }
   141	    
   142	    func numberOfItems(in gridView: FlexGridView, section: Int) -> Int {
   143	        return displayAssets.count
   144	    }
   145	    
   146	    func gridView(_ gridView: FlexGridView, viewForItemAt index: Int, section: Int, zoomLevel: ZoomLevel) -> ItemView {
   147	        guard index < displayAssets.count else {
   148	            assertionFailure("viewForItemAt index: \(index) 超出范围，displayCount: \(displayAssets.count)")
   149	            return PhotoItemView(indexPath: IndexPath(item: index, section: section))
   150	        }
   151	        
   152	        let indexPath = IndexPath(item: index, section: section)
   153	        let itemView: PhotoItemView
   154	        if let item = gridView.itemView(for: indexPath),
   155	            let v = item as? PhotoItemView {
   156	            itemView = v
   157	        } else {
   158	            itemView = PhotoItemView(indexPath: indexPath)
   159	        }
   160	
   161	        // 获取 itemSize 用于计算请求尺寸
   162	        let itemSize = gridView.itemSize(for: zoomLevel)
   163	        
   164	        // 传入 zoomLevel 和 itemSize，支持渐进式加载
   165	        itemView.configure(with: displayAssets[index], zoomLevel: zoomLevel, itemSize: itemSize)
   166	        
   167	        // 恢复选择态（如果该 item 之前被选中）
   168	        let isSelected = selectedIndices.contains(indexPath)
   169	        itemView.setSelected(isSelected)
   170	        
   171	        return itemView
   172	    }
   173	    
   174	    func gridView(_ gridView: FlexGridView, headerViewAt section: Int, zoomLevel: ZoomLevel) -> ItemHeaderView {
   175	        assert(section < sectionCount(in: gridView), "headerViewAt section: \(section) 超出范围，sectionCount: \(sectionCount(in: gridView))")
   176	        return ItemHeaderView()
   177	    }
   178	}
   179	
   180	// MARK: - FlexGridViewDelegate
   181	extension PhotoViewController: FlexGridViewDelegate {
   182	    func gridView(_ gridView: FlexGridView, didTapItemAt index: Int, section: Int) {
   183	        // 如果处于选择模式，切换该 item 的选择状态
   184	        if gridView.isSelectionMode {
   185	            let indexPath = IndexPath(item: index, section: section)
   186	            guard let itemView = gridView.itemView(for: indexPath) as? PhotoItemView else {
   187	                assertionFailure("[didChangeSelectionWithDetails] 警告: 无法获取 PhotoItemView, indexPath=\(indexPath.debugStr)")
   188	                return
   189	            }
   190	            let hidden = itemView.toggleSelected()
   191	            if !hidden {
   192	                self.selectedIndices.insert(indexPath)
   193	            }
   194	        } else {
   195	            // 非选择模式：进入详情页
   196	            presentPhotoDetail(at: index, section: section)
   197	        }
   198	    }
   199	    
   200	    
   201	    func gridView(_ gridView: FlexGridView, didDoubleTapItemAt index: Int, section: Int) {
   202	        // 确保索引有效
   203	        guard index < displayAssets.count else {
   204	            return
   205	        }
   206	        // 隐藏照片的确认弹窗（从展示中移除，不从系统删除）
   207	        showHidePhotoAlert(at: index)
   208	    }
   209	    
   210	    func gridView(_ gridView: FlexGridView, didChangeLevelTo level: ZoomLevel) {
   211	        // Level 切换后，取消之前的低优先级请求
   212	        ImageRequestManager.shared.cancelRequests(belowOrEqualPriority: .normal)
   213	        
   214	        // 获取当前屏幕可见内容并请求高清图
   215	        let currentVisibleItems = gridView.currentVisibleItemIndices()
   216	        
   217	        Logger.log("Update") { "[LevelChange] Level切换到 \(level), 可见: \(currentVisibleItems.count)" }
   218	        
   219	        requestHighResForVisibleItems(currentVisibleItems, priority: .high)
   220	    }
   221	    
   222	    /// - Parameters:
   223	    ///   - addedIndices: 新增选中的索引集合
   224	    ///   - removedIndices: 移除选中的索引集合
   225	    ///   - allSelectedIndices: 当前所有选中的索引集合
   226	    func gridView(_ gridView: FlexGridView, didChangeSelectionWithDetails addedIndices: Set<IndexPath>, removedIndices: Set<IndexPath>, allSelectedIndices: Set<IndexPath>) {
   227	        // 合并所有变化的索引，统一处理
   228	        let changedIndices = addedIndices.union(removedIndices)
   229	        for indexPath in changedIndices {
   230	            guard let itemView = gridView.itemView(for: indexPath) as? PhotoItemView else {
   231	                assertionFailure("[didChangeSelectionWithDetails] 警告: 无法获取 PhotoItemView, indexPath=\(indexPath.debugStr)")
   232	                continue
   233	            }
   234	            let hidden = itemView.toggleSelected()
   235	            if !hidden {
   236	                self.selectedIndices.insert(indexPath)
   237	            }
   238	        }
   239	    }
   240	    
   241	    /// 滑动删除触发时调用
   242	    func gridView(_ gridView: FlexGridView, didSwipeToDeleteItemAt index: Int, section: Int) {
   243	        Logger.log("delete") { "[PhotoViewController] 滑动删除触发: index=\(index)" }
   244	        
   245	        // 检查索引有效性
   246	        guard index < displayAssets.count else {
   247	            assertionFailure("滑动删除索引越界: \(index), count=\(displayAssets.count)")
   248	            return
   249	        }
   250	        
   251	        // 复用现有的 hidePhoto 逻辑
   252	        hidePhoto(at: index)
   253	        
   254	        // 通知过滤协调器照片被删除
   255	        filterCoordinator?.handleAssetHidden(at: index)
   256	    }
   257	    
   258	    /// 长按触发时调用
   259	    func gridView(_ gridView: FlexGridView, didLongPressItemAt index: Int, section: Int) {
   260	        Logger.log("filter") { "[PhotoViewController] 长按触发: index=\(index)" }
   261	        
   262	        // 检查索引有效性
   263	        guard index < displayAssets.count else { return }
   264	        
   265	        let asset = displayAssets[index]
   266	        let indexPath = IndexPath(item: index, section: section)
   267	        
   268	        // 通知过滤协调器
   269	        filterCoordinator?.handleLongPress(on: asset, at: indexPath)
   270	    }
   271	    
   272	    /// 滚动停止时调用，按优先级请求图片
   273	    /// P0: 当前屏幕可见内容（最高优先级）
   274	    /// P1: 临近屏幕内容
   275	    /// P2: 缩略图预加载（最低优先级）
   276	    func gridView(_ gridView: FlexGridView, didEndScrolling offset: CGPoint) {
   277	        
   278	        // 取消之前未完成的低优先级请求（新的滚动停止事件触发）
   279	        ImageRequestManager.shared.cancelRequests(belowOrEqualPriority: .normal)
   280	        
   281	        // P0: 获取当前屏幕可见的内容（screenCount=0 表示仅当前屏幕）
   282	        let currentVisibleItems = gridView.currentVisibleItemIndices()
   283	        
   284	        // P1: 获取临近屏幕的内容（根据 level 决定预加载屏数）
   285	        let screenCount: Int = gridView.currentLevel == .level1 ? 2 : 1
   286	        let adjacentItems = gridView.adjacentItemIndices(screenCount: screenCount)
   287	        
   288	        Logger.log("Update") { "[Preload] 滚动停止，可见: \(currentVisibleItems.count), 临近: \(adjacentItems.count)" }
   289	        
   290	        // P0: 优先请求当前屏幕可见的高清图
   291	        requestHighResForVisibleItems(currentVisibleItems, priority: .high) { [weak self] in
   292	            guard let self = self else { return }
   293	            
   294	            // P1: 当前屏幕完成后，请求临近屏幕的高清图
   295	            self.requestHighResForVisibleItems(adjacentItems, priority: .normal) { [weak self] in
   296	                guard let self = self else { return }
   297	                
   298	                // P2: 最后预加载缩略图
   299	                let maxLoadedIndex = (currentVisibleItems + adjacentItems).map { $0.item }.max() ?? 0
   300	                if maxLoadedIndex < self.displayAssets.count - 1 {
   301	                    self.preloadThumbnails(startIndex: maxLoadedIndex + 1)
   302	                }
   303	            }
   304	        }
   305	    }
   306	}
   307	
   308	extension PhotoViewController {
   309	    func clearSelectionStatus() {
   310	        guard gridView.isSelectionMode == false else {
   311	            return
   312	        }
   313	        
   314	        for indexPath in self.selectedIndices {
   315	            guard let itemView = gridView.itemView(for: indexPath) as? PhotoItemView else {
   316	                Logger.log("selection") {"\(indexPath.debugStr) is remove from gridview"}
   317	                continue
   318	            }
   319	            itemView.toggleSelected()
   320	        }
   321	        self.selectedIndices.removeAll()
   322	    }
   323	    
   324	    // MARK: - Thumbnail Preload (启动时/滑动中调用)
   325	    
   326	    /// 批量预加载缩略图
   327	    /// - Parameter startIndex: 起始索引
   328	    /// - Parameter count: 预加载数量
   329	    func preloadThumbnails(startIndex: Int = 0, count: Int? = nil) {
   330	        let batchSize = count ?? ImageCacheConfig.thumbnailBatchSize
   331	        let endIndex = min(startIndex + batchSize, displayAssets.count)
   332	        
   333	        guard startIndex < endIndex else { return }
   334	        
   335	        let modelsToPreload = Array(displayAssets[startIndex..<endIndex])
   336	        
   337	        let batchStartTime = CFAbsoluteTimeGetCurrent()
   338	        Logger.log("preload") { "[Preload] 开始批量预加载缩略图: startIndex=\(startIndex), count=\(modelsToPreload.count)" }
   339	        
   340	        ImageRequestManager.shared.requestThumbnailsBatch(for: modelsToPreload) { successCount in
   341	            let elapsed = (CFAbsoluteTimeGetCurrent() - batchStartTime) * 1000
   342	            let avgTime = successCount > 0 ? elapsed / Double(successCount) : 0
   343	            Logger.log("preload") { "[Preload] 缩略图预加载完成: \(successCount) 张, 总耗时=\(String(format: "%.2f", elapsed))ms, 平均=\(String(format: "%.2f", avgTime))ms/张" }
   344	        }
   345	    }
   346	    
   347	    // MARK: - High-Res Request (滚动停止后调用)
   348	    
   349	    /// 请求可见区域的高清图（带优先级和完成回调）
   350	    /// - Parameters:
   351	    ///   - visibleIndices: 可见区域的索引数组
   352	    ///   - priority: 请求优先级
   353	    ///   - completion: 批次完成回调，用于链式触发下一优先级请求
   354	    private func requestHighResForVisibleItems(
   355	        _ visibleIndices: [IndexPath],
   356	        priority: ImageRequestPriority = .normal,
   357	        completion: (() -> Void)? = nil
   358	    ) {
   359	        guard !visibleIndices.isEmpty else {
   360	            completion?()
   361	            return
   362	        }
   363	        
   364	        let zoomLevel = gridView.currentLevel
   365	        let itemSize = gridView.itemSize(for: zoomLevel)
   366	        let scale = UIScreen.main.scale
   367	        let targetSize = CGSize(width: itemSize.width * scale, height: itemSize.height * scale)
   368	        
   369	        // 收集需要请求高清的 AssetModel（过滤掉已显示足够清晰图片的 item）
   370	        var modelsToRequest: [AssetModel] = []
   371	        var skippedCount = 0
   372	        
   373	        for indexPath in visibleIndices {
   374	            guard indexPath.item >= 0, indexPath.item < displayAssets.count else { continue }
   375	            
   376	            let assetModel = displayAssets[indexPath.item]
   377	            
   378	            // 检查当前 itemView 显示的图片是否已足够清晰
   379	            if let itemView = gridView.itemView(for: indexPath) as? PhotoItemView,
   380	               let currentImage = itemView.imageView.image {
   381	                let currentImageSize = currentImage.size
   382	                // 如果当前图片尺寸已 >= 目标尺寸的 80%，认为足够清晰，跳过请求
   383	                if currentImageSize.width >= targetSize.width * 0.8 &&
   384	                   currentImageSize.height >= targetSize.height * 0.8 {
   385	                    skippedCount += 1
   386	                    continue
   387	                }
   388	            }
   389	            
   390	            modelsToRequest.append(assetModel)
   391	        }
   392	        
   393	        if skippedCount > 0 {
   394	            Logger.log("HighRes") { "[Update] 跳过已清晰图片: \(skippedCount) 张" }
   395	        }
   396	        
   397	        guard !modelsToRequest.isEmpty else {
   398	            Logger.log("HighRes") { "[Update] 所有可见图片已足够清晰，无需请求高清图，优先级=\(priority.description)" }
   399	            completion?()
   400	            return
   401	        }
   402	        
   403	        let batchStartTime = CFAbsoluteTimeGetCurrent()
   404	        Logger.log("HighRes") { "[Update] 开始请求高清图: \(modelsToRequest.count) 张, 优先级=\(priority.description), targetSize=\(targetSize.debugStr)" }
   405	        
   406	        // 批量请求高清图（带优先级）
   407	        ImageRequestManager.shared.requestHighResBatch(
   408	            for: modelsToRequest,
   409	            targetSize: targetSize,
   410	            priority: priority,
   411	            perImageCompletion: { [weak self] assetId, image in
   412	                guard let self = self, let image = image else { return }
   413	                
   414	                // 找到对应的 itemView 并更新高清图
   415	                self.updateHighResForAsset(assetId: assetId, image: image)
   416	            },
   417	            batchCompletion: { successCount, totalCount in
   418	                let elapsed = (CFAbsoluteTimeGetCurrent() - batchStartTime) * 1000
   419	                let avgTime = successCount > 0 ? elapsed / Double(successCount) : 0
   420	                Logger.log("HighRes") { "[Update] 高清图请求完成[\(priority.description)]: \(successCount)/\(totalCount) 张, 总耗时=\(String(format: "%.2f", elapsed))ms, 平均=\(String(format: "%.2f", avgTime))ms/张" }
   421	                
   422	                // 触发下一优先级请求
   423	                completion?()
   424	            }
   425	        )
   426	    }
   427	    
   428	    /// 更新指定 asset 的高清图
   429	    private func updateHighResForAsset(assetId: String, image: UIImage) {
   430	        // 找到 asset 对应的 indexPath
   431	        guard let index = displayAssets.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == assetId }) else { return }
   432	        
   433	        let indexPath = IndexPath(item: index, section: 0)
   434	        
   435	        // 获取 itemView 并更新
   436	        guard let itemView = gridView.itemView(for: indexPath) as? PhotoItemView else { return }
   437	        
   438	        itemView.imageView.image = image
   439	        
   440	        Logger.log("HighRes") { "[Update] 高清图更新到 UI: assetId=\(assetId), indexPath=\(indexPath.debugStr)" }
   441	    }
   442	    
   443	    // MARK: - First Screen Load (首屏加载)
   444	    /// 加载首屏内容（高清图 + 触发缩略图批量预加载）
   445	    func loadCurrentScreenImage() {
   446	        // 1. 获取首屏可见索引
   447	        let visibleIndices = gridView.currentVisibleItemIndices()
   448	        
   449	        guard !visibleIndices.isEmpty else {
   450	            Logger.log("preload") { "[Preload] 首屏加载跳过，无可见项" }
   451	            return
   452	        }
   453	        
   454	        Logger.log("preload") { "[Preload] 首屏加载开始: \(visibleIndices.count) 个可见项" }
   455	        
   456	        // 2. 请求首屏高清图
   457	        requestHighResForVisibleItems(visibleIndices)
   458	        
   459	        // 3. 启动批量缩略图预加载（后台进行）
   460	        DispatchQueue.main.asyncAfter(deadline: .now() + 0.1) { [weak self] in
   461	            self?.preloadThumbnails()
   462	        }
   463	    }
   464	}
   465	
   466	extension PhotoViewController {
   467	    
   468	    /// 进入照片详情页
   469	    private func presentPhotoDetail(at index: Int, section: Int) {
   470	        
   471	        guard index < displayAssets.count else { return }
   472	        
   473	        let indexPath = IndexPath(item: index, section: section)
   474	        
   475	        // 获取点击的 itemView
   476	        guard let itemView = gridView.itemView(for: indexPath) as? PhotoItemView else {
   477	            assertionFailure("[PhotoViewController] 无法获取 PhotoItemView, 直接进入详情页")
   478	            return
   479	        }
   480	        
   481	        // 获取 itemView 在 window 中的位置
   482	        let sourceFrame = itemView.convert(itemView.bounds, to: view.window)
   483	        
   484	        // 获取当前显示的图片
   485	        let sourceImage = itemView.imageView.image
   486	        
   487	        // 创建详情页
   488	        let detailVC = DetailViewController(
   489	            assets: displayAssets,
   490	            initialIndex: index,
   491	            sourceFrame: sourceFrame,
   492	            sourceImage: sourceImage
   493	        )
   494	        
   495	    
   496	        // 返回时的回调
   497	        detailVC.onDismiss = { [weak self] deletedAssets, currentIndex in
   498	            guard let self = self else { return }
   499	            
   500	            // 1. 根据删除的内容做无动画删除
   501	            if !deletedAssets.isEmpty {
   502	                self.handleDeletedAssetsFromDetail(deletedAssets)
   503	            }
   504	            
   505	            // 2. 根据 currentIndex 判断是否需要滚动
   506	            self.scrollToItemIfNeeded(at: currentIndex)
   507	            
   508	            Logger.log(.all) { "[PhotoViewController] 详情页返回, deletedCount=\(deletedAssets.count), currentIndex=\(currentIndex)" }
   509	            self.loadCurrentScreenImage()
   510	        }
   511	        
   512	        // 获取 dismiss 动画的目标 frame
   513	        detailVC.getTargetFrameForDismiss = { [weak self] currentIndex in
   514	            guard let self = self else { return .zero }
   515	            return self.getTargetFrameForItem(at: currentIndex)
   516	        }
   517	        
   518	        // 弹出详情页（高清图由详情页内部请求）
   519	        present(detailVC, animated: true)
   520	    }
   521	    
   522	    /// 获取指定索引 item 的目标 frame（用于 dismiss 转场动画）
   523	    /// 滚动已在 onDismiss 回调中处理完成，这里直接获取 item 在 window 中的 frame
   524	    private func getTargetFrameForItem(at index: Int) -> CGRect {
   525	        let indexPath = IndexPath(item: index, section: 0)
   526	        
   527	        // 获取 item 在 window 中的 frame
   528	        guard let itemView = gridView.itemView(for: indexPath) else {
   529	            Logger.log(.all) { "[PhotoViewController] getTargetFrameForItem 无法获取 itemView, index=\(index)" }
   530	            return .zero
   531	        }
   532	        
   533	        let frameInWindow = itemView.convert(itemView.bounds, to: view.window)
   534	        Logger.log(.all) { "[PhotoViewController] getTargetFrameForItem index=\(index) frameInWindow=\(frameInWindow.debugStr)" }
   535	        return frameInWindow
   536	    }
   537	    
   538	    // MARK: - Detail Dismiss Helpers
   539	    
   540	    /// 处理从详情页返回时删除的 assets（无动画删除）
   541	    private func handleDeletedAssetsFromDetail(_ deletedAssets: [AssetModel]) {
   542	        var deleteIndexPaths: [IndexPath] = []
   543	        var indicesToRemove: [Int] = []
   544	        
   545	        for (index, asset) in displayAssets.enumerated().reversed() {
   546	            if deletedAssets.contains(where: { $0.id == asset.id }) {
   547	                deleteIndexPaths.append(IndexPath(item: index, section: 0))
   548	                indicesToRemove.append(index)
   549	            }
   550	        }
   551	        
   552	        // 从 displayAssets 中移除
   553	        for index in indicesToRemove.sorted(by: >) {
   554	            displayAssets.remove(at: index)
   555	        }
   556	        
   557	        // 无动画更新 UI
   558	        if !deleteIndexPaths.isEmpty {
   559	            gridView.deleteItems(at: deleteIndexPaths, animated: false)
   560	        }
   561	        
   562	        Logger.log(.all) { "[PhotoViewController] handleDeletedAssetsFromDetail: 删除 \(deleteIndexPaths.count) 个 items" }
   563	    }
   564	    
   565	    /// 根据 item 在屏幕的位置决定是否需要滚动
   566	    /// - 如果 item.top 在合适范围内 [screenHeight/2, screenHeight - itemHeight - bottomSafeArea]，不滚动
   567	    /// - 否则将 item 移动到屏幕 2/3 处（考虑 contentOffset 边界限制）
   568	    private func scrollToItemIfNeeded(at index: Int) {
   569	        guard index >= 0, index < displayAssets.count else { return }
   570	        
   571	        let indexPath = IndexPath(item: index, section: 0)
   572	        let level = gridView.currentLevel
   573	        
   574	        guard let itemFrame = gridView.itemFrame(index: indexPath, level: level) else { return }
   575	        
   576	        let screenHeight = gridView.bounds.height
   577	        let currentOffset = gridView.currentOffset.y
   578	        let itemSize = gridView.itemSize(for: level)
   579	        let bottomSafeArea = view.safeAreaInsets.bottom
   580	        
   581	        // 计算 item.top 在当前屏幕中的 Y 位置
   582	        let itemTopInScreen = itemFrame.minY - currentOffset
   583	        
   584	        // 合适范围：[screenHeight/2, screenHeight - itemHeight - bottomSafeArea]
   585	        let comfortableTop = screenHeight * 0.4
   586	        let comfortableBottom = screenHeight - itemSize.height - bottomSafeArea
   587	        
   588	        // 判断 item.top 是否在合适范围内
   589	        let isInComfortableRange = itemTopInScreen >= comfortableTop && itemTopInScreen <= comfortableBottom
   590	        
   591	        if isInComfortableRange {
   592	            Logger.log(.all) { "[PhotoViewController] scrollToItemIfNeeded: item 在合适范围内，不滚动. itemTopInScreen=\(itemTopInScreen.debugStr), range=[\(comfortableTop.debugStr), \(comfortableBottom.debugStr)]" }
   593	            return
   594	        }
   595	        
   596	        // 计算目标位置：item 中心位于屏幕 2/3 处
   597	        let targetCenterY = screenHeight * 2 / 3
   598	        let targetTopY = targetCenterY - itemSize.height / 2
   599	        
   600	        let targetFrameInScreen = CGRect(
   601	            x: 0,
   602	            y: targetTopY,
   603	            width: itemSize.width,
   604	            height: itemSize.height
   605	        )
   606	        
   607	        // 使用 FlexGridView 的方法计算 offset（会自动 clamp 到有效范围）
   608	        let targetOffset = gridView.offsetForItemRectInScreen(
   609	            for: indexPath,
   610	            level: level,
   611	            frameInScreen: targetFrameInScreen
   612	        )
   613	        
   614	        Logger.log(.all) { "[PhotoViewController] scrollToItemIfNeeded: 滚动到 index=\(index), targetOffset=\(targetOffset.debugStr)" }
   615	        
   616	        // 无动画滚动
   617	        gridView.setContentOffset(CGPoint(x: 0, y: targetOffset), animated: false)
   618	        gridView.layoutIfNeeded()
   619	    }
   620	}


</details>

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

我已经有足够的信息来理解问题并设计解决方案了。

从代码中可以看到：

1. **当前错误逻辑**（第 357-376 行）：
   - 使用 `location.y > screenHeight - 150` 来判断是否在底部区域
   - 这意味着用户必须在屏幕物理底部 150pt 区域内滑动才会触发

2. **正确逻辑应该是**：
   - 用户先滚动到 gridView 的最底部（即 `gridView.currentOffset.y` 接近最大可滚动距离）
   - 然后继续向下拖拽（overscroll）时才触发手势

3. **关键信息**：
   - `gridView.currentOffset` 是 CGPoint，表示当前滚动位置
   - `gridView.bounds.height` 是 gridView 的高度
   - `gridView` 应该有一个方法来计算内容高度，或者可以通过 `gridView.setContentOffset` 来设置

但是我需要知道如何计算内容高度（contentSize.height）。让我检查一下是否有 `contentSize` 或类似属性。

由于 `FlexGridView` 似乎是外部库，我需要假设它的 API。从代码中可以看到：
- `gridView.currentOffset` - 当前滚动偏移
- `gridView.setContentOffset(_:animated:)` - 设置滚动偏移
- `gridView.bounds.height` - gridView 高度

但是我还需要知道内容总高度才能判断是否滚动到底部。

让我搜索一下是否有其他方式获取内容高度或者可以监听滚动到底部的事件。

</details>

    18	// MARK: - FlexGridView
    19	public class FlexGridView: UIView {
    20	    
    21	    // MARK: - Public Properties
    22	    public weak var dataSource: FlexGridViewDataSource?
    23	    public weak var delegate: FlexGridViewDelegate?
    24	    /// 配置信息
    25	    public var config: FlexGridViewConfig = FlexGridViewConfig()
    26	    /// 是否处于多选模式（外部控制）
    27	    public var isSelectionMode: Bool = false {
    28	        didSet {
    29	            if isSelectionMode != oldValue {
    30	                handleSelectionModeChanged()
    31	            }
    32	        }
    33	    }
    34	    
    35	    // MARK: - Readonly Properties
    36	    let containerView = CustomContainerView()
    37	    /// 当前档位（对外只读）
    38	    public private(set) var currentLevel: ZoomLevel = .defaultLevel
    39	    /// 是否正在滚动（对外只读，用于手势协调）
    40	    public private(set) var isScrolling: Bool = false
    41	    
    42	    // MARK: - Inner Properties
    43	    /// Reload时更新
    44	    /// indexPath.section : 当前section
    45	    /// indexPath.item : 当前section中item的个数，非item的索引
    46	    var itemIndexes: [IndexPath] = []
    47	    /// 可见区域的item视图字典：index -> ItemView
    48	    /// 这里的可视区域不是仅屏幕内容，而是所有已经添加到FlexGridView上的ItemView
    49	    var visibleItemViews: [IndexPath: ItemView] = [:]
    50	    /// 可见区域的header视图字典：section -> ItemHeaderView
    51	    var visibleHeaderViews: [Int: ItemHeaderView] = [:]
    52	    
    53	    // MARK: - Private Properties
    54	    /// 用于提供 pan 手势的不可见 UIScrollView
    55	    let flexScrollView = FlexScrollView()
    56	    /// item size缓存：level -> size
    57	    private var itemSizeCache: [ZoomLevel: CGSize] = [:]
    58	    /// contentHeight缓存：level -> height
    59	    var contentHeightCache: [ZoomLevel: CGFloat] = [:]
    60	    /// 缓存bounds.width，用于检测视图width变化
    61	    private var cachedWidth: CGFloat = 0
    62	    private var didLayout = false
    63	
    64	    // MARK: - Cache
    65	    func invalidateContentHeightCache() {
    66	        contentHeightCache.removeAll()
    67	    }
    68	    
    69	    // MARK: - 捏合手势状态
    70	    var pinchStatus: PinchStatus? = nil
    71	    
    72	    // MARK: - Selection Mode Properties

    75

    83	        let startLocation: CGPoint

   119	        super.init(coder: coder)
